July 20th, 1993 - Washington D.C, 1600 Pennsylvania Ave

Hillary felt happy, relieved. That snake was finally going to be killed today. She had been planning this for months — and tonight her efforts would finally bear fruit. He cannot be allowed to survive, no matter the price. She had even recorded herself ordering his death, so she could look back and laugh at it later.

It didn't matter that she had worked with him for years, or that he had helped her become a lawyer in the first place. All that matters is that she must protect herself. She has no other choice.

She had done stuff typical of a First Lady today — giving speeches, attending schools, making millions illegally for her own pleasure. Sitting on the White House couch, flicking through meaningless television channels, she began to get worried. Had the plan failed? Had that rat managed to get away?

Just then, someone knocked on the door. It was the agents tasked with killing him.

“Target neutralized, Madame'.”

Grinning, she replied “Excellent.”

“And did you get that tape I asked for?” Hillary really hoped they recorded it. She would get to watch that loser die in real time, entertainment far beyond her wildest dreams.

“Of course” an agent replied.

“Perfect!” she said, trying her best to contain her excitement.

She quickly ran to the oven and put in a batch of chocolate-chip cookies. If she was quick, she and Bill could even get a midnight snack to go alongside her night-time entertainment.

She called her husband downstairs as she put the tape inside the television. Bill laughed, and she cackled. They couldn't stop replaying the 2 hour long video of his suffering. They dragged him all the way to Virginia and shot the bastard dead.

Just then her advisors walked in. They had already written a script for her to say when she “learns” of Foster's death, and already wrote an eulogy for Bill to say at his funeral. Hillary said she couldn't be bothered to attend, just make up some excuse about her being sick that day. The press was already at the White House that night, and she feigned horror, crying about how tragic it was. The media used it as ''proof'' of her humbleness.

The entire cabinet was far too spineless to ever report her crimes. Spinelessness was a trait Clinton always looked for in cabinet appointments, and she always made sure her crimes never got in contact with people who still had some of their guts left.

The brutality of her acts stimulated her. It made her satisfied, fulfilled, relieved. This was the best smile she's had in years. Apart from wearing fancy dresses, it was her favorite coping mechanism.

Just then, midnight struck, it was their bedtime. She called Bill upstairs, and they slept soundly in the White House bedroom, knowing they would never have to bear the consequences of their actions.

August 17th, 2018 - Federal Bureau of Investigation catches Hillary Clinton in New York | Syracuse Register

This article has been updated to include further details.

The former First Lady and 2016 presidential candidate has been on the run for years ever since an anonymous person leaked a video clip of her ordering her the murder of Vince Foster. That changed today, where the FBI coordinated with local authorities and the state of Virginia to capture Clinton, who had been hiding in a mansion in upstate New York.

Raiding her home, she quickly surrendered. Authorities found she was armed with weapons and had written a note about fleeing to Canada.

The whereabouts of her husband Bill Clinton are unknown, though she was still wearing her wedding ring when she was caught, and she appeared to be living in luxury, with many amenities.

Given the murder of Foster was successful, she could be tried for first degree murder under Virginia law. Prosecutors say they will try to push for the death penalty. Former President Barack Obama condemned Clinton harshly in a post on Twitter, saying “I once called Hillary Clinton a friend. But after what she did, I can't even bare to look at her anymore. I unequivocally denounce her, and I hope she will be prosecuted to the fullest extent under law.“

The death penalty is still legal under Virginia law, though opposition has been mounting, as of late. She will be extradited to the police of Fairfax County, Virginia.

This article was written by Shamar Marco.

November 21st, 2020 - Court sentences Hillary Clinton to death - Newsmax

It's not looking good for Hillary Clinton.

The former First Lady, Senator, Secretary of State and 2016 presidential candidate Hillary Clinton was recently found guilty of the murder of Vince Foster, and sentenced to death. A trail of phone calls, video tapes, confessions, and clear evidence has led to the jury and judge sentencing her to execution via lethal injection.

Hillary Rodham Clinton has continued to profess her innocence, but her legal team, despite being very prestigious, has struggled to find good routes of defense. The system also railroaded her execution date to just 1 year from now, in 2020. Virginia Governor Ralph Northam has been neutral in the endeavor, though his ally Terry McAullife, has been strongly opposed, and has even called on Governor Northam to pardon Clinton.

This revalation is a major turning point in the accountability of our government. When asked about it on Saturday, President-elect Bernie Sanders said ''I believe the political violence that Clinton engaged in was despicable. That said, the solution to violence is not violence. I oppose the death penalty, and I believe she should be given a life sentence. Furthermore, I urge her to reveal who else was behind these crimes.'' Clinton has still refused to do so.

Updated 12/5/2020

Hillary Clinton - Wikipedia

Hillary Diane Rodham Clinton (October 26, 1947 - December 9th, 2021) was an American politician who served as the Secretary of State of the United States of America from 2009 to 2013. She is also a former Democratic member of the U.S. Senate from the state of New York. Clinton served in the Senate from 2001 to 2009. She was the first former First Lady to serve in the U.S. Senate and in a president's cabinet.

In 2016, Hillary Clinton was exposed for murder and fraud. She was apprehended by authorities in 2018, and following a long legal battle, executed in 2021. A bill banning the death penalty in Virginia passed soon after her execution. Governor Ralph Northam declined to make a comment, whilst Governor-elect Glenn Youngkin did not comment on her execution but called her actions ''disgusting.'' Her husband Bill Clinton was sentenced to 10 years in prison for fraud and conspiracy to murder.
